# orphanet

This document details the invalid local unique identifiers used in CURIEs
for node, synonym, and definition cross-references in `orphanet`.


## `Genatlas`: Genatlas

Overall, there were 49 invalid
xrefs to external prefixed with `Genatlas` (standardized to Bioregistry
prefix [`genatlas`](https://bioregistry.io/genatlas)) that
did not match the standard pattern `^\w+$`.
